Lab #4 - Data Wrangling¶

Exercise #1¶

Step 1.1.a¶

The class is "wikitable".¶

Step 1.1.b¶

In [155]:
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
wiki_url = 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_natural_satellites'
# Request the http page
wiki_page = requests.get(wiki_url)
# Pas the text of the webpage recieved from the request to the parser
wiki_page_soup = BeautifulSoup(wiki_page.text, 'html.parser')
# Find all tables which has a class "wikitable"
wiki_page_list = wiki_page_soup.find_all(name="table", class_="wikitable")
print("The number of tables with class \"wikitable\" are - ", len(wiki_page_list))

The number of tables with class "wikitable" are -  5

Step 1.1.c¶

The table we are interested in is at index 4.¶

In [156]:
# Entry of the table of interest from the list

Step 2.2¶

In [162]:
import numpy as np
# Clean the 'Numeral' column by removing everything but the integer value
wiki_table['Numeral'] = wiki_table['Numeral'].str.extract(pat = '(\d+)')
# Convert the data type from object to int
wiki_table['Numeral'] = pd.to_numeric(wiki_table['Numeral'])
# Remove the NaN values from the column
wiki_table['Numeral'] = wiki_table['Numeral'].replace(np.nan, 0)

Exercise #3¶

What is the total number of satellites that each parent has? Which parent has the largest and the smallest number of satellites?¶

In [163]:
wiki_table.groupby(['Parent Planet'])['Numeral'].max()
Out[163]:
Parent Planet
Earth        1.0
Eris         1.0
Haumea       2.0
Jupiter     72.0
Makemake     0.0
Mars         2.0
Neptune     14.0
Pluto        5.0
Saturn      53.0
Uranus      27.0
Name: Numeral, dtype: float64

The total number of satellites for each parent is shown above. Jupiter has the largest number of satellites whereas Makemake has the smallest number of satellites.¶

In [ ]:
